     <h2 id="post-60">
      <a href="http://dallasvintageshop.com/vintage-sunglasses/" rel="bookmark" title="Permanent Link to Vintage Sunglasses">
       Vintage Sunglasses
      </a>
     </h2>
     <!-- 
original little date tag
&lt;small&gt;January 13th, 2008 
-->
     <!-- by kry &lt;/small&gt;

     <div class="entry">
      <p class="narrowcolumn" id="content">
      </p>
      <p class="post">
       Horn rims-dozens or styles and colors, including polkadots clear or tinted lenses, checkerboards, rhinestones, pearlized, oversized, neons, nerdy, amazing or sophisticated. The same in hippie, John Lennons. We have glasses and sunglasses for Ben Franklin, FDR, John Kennedy, Buddy Holly, Clark Kent, Bessy Ross, Blues Brothers, Cops, bikers, Elvis, Willy Wonka, and so much more. Goggles-there are so many kinds of goggles and weve got them.

     <h2 id="post-8994">
      <a href="http://dallasvintageshop.com/warning-dallas-vintage-shop-has-true-pedigree-vintage-attire-however-we-also-provide-fancy-theme-party-costumes-for-any-decade-century-or-theme-we-dont-claim-to-be-the-typical-vintage-boutique/" rel="bookmark" title="Permanent Link to WARNING: Dallas Vintage Shop has true pedigree vintage attire. However, we also provide fancy theme party costumes for any decade, century or theme. We dont claim to be the typical vintage boutique. Although we have enormous quantities of amazing vintage, we also provide theme party costumes with the, Wow! factor. Some people prefer vintage, but many prefer new. Therefore, we have quality replicas and costumes in vast quantities in a gigantic variety of styles with a large range of sizes.">
       WARNING: Dallas Vintage Shop has true pedigree vintage attire. However, we also provide fancy theme party costumes for any decade, century or theme. We dont claim to be the typical vintage boutique. Although we have enormous quantities of amazing vintage, we also provide theme party costumes with the, Wow! factor. Some people prefer vintage, but many prefer new. Therefore, we have quality replicas and costumes in vast quantities in a gigantic variety of styles with a large range of sizes.
      </a>
     </h2>
     <!-- 
original little date tag
&lt;small&gt;June 22nd, 2004 
-->
